Sets a maximum width relative to the parent and auto scales the height\\n * 2. Corrects `max-width` behavior if padding and border are used\\n *\\/\\n\\naudio,\\ncanvas,\\nimg,\\nsvg,\\nvideo {\\n    \\/* 1 *\\/\\n    max-width: 100%;\\n    height: auto;\\n    \\/* 2 *\\/\\n    box-sizing: border-box;\\n}\\n\\n\\/*\\n * Preserve original dimensions\\n *\\/\\n\\n.uk-img-preserve,\\n.uk-img-preserve audio,\\n.uk-img-preserve canvas,\\n.uk-img-preserve img,\\n.uk-img-preserve svg,\\n.uk-img-preserve video { max-width: none; }\\n\\n* + p,\\n* + ul,\\n* + ol,\\n* + dl,\\n* + blockquote,\\n* + pre,\\n* + address,\\n* + fieldset,\\n* + figure { margin-top: @base-margin-vertical; }\\n\\n\\n\\/* Headings\\n ========================================================================== *\\/\\n\\nh1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6 {\\n    margin: 0 0 @base-margin-vertical 0;\\n    font-family:  @base-heading-font-family;\\n    font-weight: @base-heading-font-weight;\\n    color: @base-heading-color;\\n    text-transform: @base-heading-text-transform;\\n    .hook-base-h;\\n}\\n\\n\\/*\\n * Margins\\n *\\/\\n\\n* + h1,\\n* + h2,\\n* + h3,\\n* + h4,\\n* + h5,\\n* + h6 { margin-top: @base-heading-margin-top;
